(*****************************************************************************************

 Pseudo double category to Verity double bicategory

 Every pseudo double category `C` gives rise to a Verity double bicategory. This Verity
 double bicategory is defined as follows:
 - Objects: objects in `C`
 - Horizontal 1-cells: vertical morphisms in `C`
 - Horizontal 2-cells: equalities of vertical morphisms
 - Vertical 1-cells: horizontal morphisms in `C`
 - Vertical 2-cells: globular squares in `C`
 - Squares: squares in `C`
 Note that the horizontal and vertical morphisms get swapped in this construction. For
 Verity double bicategories, this does not matter, because their definition is symmetric.
 The reason why this swap is desired, is because for Verity double bicategories and for
 pseudo double categories, a different convention is used regarding which morphisms are
 called horizontal and which ones are called vertical. For Verity double bicategories,
 the PhD thesis of Verity is followed, whereas for pseudo double categories, the book on
 2-dimensional categories by Johnson and Yau is followed.

 Another thing that is worth noticing, is that vertical 2-cells correspond to
 squares in this Verity double bicategory. However, the same cannot be said for the
 horizontal 2-cells. For example, we could consider the pseudo double category whose
 objects are strict categories, vertical morphisms are categories, horizontal morphisms
 are profunctors, and whose squares are given by natural transformations. Equalities of
 functors between strict categories do not correspond to squares whose horizontal sides
 are identity profunctors.

 Contents
 1. The vertical bicategory
 2. The whiskering operations
 3. The laws of the Verity double bicategory
 4. The Verity double bicategory coming from a pseudo double category
 5. The univalence of this Verity double bicategory
 6. Companions and conjoints

 *****************************************************************************************)

Notation "_ ≠ _" was already used in scope nat_scope.

C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
∏
(w x y
 z : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_bicat_ver_id_comp)
(h₁ : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_bicat_ver_id_comp
      ⟦ w, x ⟧)
(h₂ : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_bicat_ver_id_comp
      ⟦ y, z ⟧)
(v₁
 v₁' : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
         double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_bicat_ver_id_comp
       ⟦ w, y ⟧)
(v₂ : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
        double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_bicat_ver_id_comp
      ⟦ x, z ⟧),
v₁ ==> v₁'
→ square_double_bicat h₁ h₂ v₁' v₂
  → square_double_bicat h₁ h₂ v₁ v₂
 exact (λ (w x y z : C)
               (v₁ : w -->v x) (v₂ : y -->v z)
               (h₁ h₁' : w -->h y) (h₂ : x -->h z)
               (s₁ : square (identity_v w) (identity_v y) h₁ h₁')
               (s₂ : square v₁ v₂ h₁' h₂),
             transportf_square
               (id_v_left _)
               (id_v_left _)
               (s₁ ⋆v s₂)).
    
C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
∏
(w x y
 z : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_bicat_ver_id_comp)
(h₁ : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_bicat_ver_id_comp
      ⟦ w, x ⟧)
(h₂ : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_bicat_ver_id_comp
      ⟦ y, z ⟧)
(v₁ : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
        double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_bicat_ver_id_comp
      ⟦ w, y ⟧)
(v₂
 v₂' : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
         double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_bicat_ver_id_comp
       ⟦ x, z ⟧),
v₂ ==> v₂'
→ square_double_bicat h₁ h₂ v₁ v₂
  → square_double_bicat h₁ h₂ v₁ v₂'
 exact (λ (w x y z : C)
               (v₁ : w -->v x) (v₂ : y -->v z)
               (h₁ : w -->h y) (h₂ h₂' : x -->h z)
               (s₁ : square (identity_v _) (identity_v _) h₂ h₂')
               (s₂ : square v₁ v₂ h₁ h₂),
             transportf_square
               (id_v_right _)
               (id_v_right _)
               (s₂ ⋆v s₁)).
    
C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
∏
(w x y
 z : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_bicat_ver_id_comp)
(h₁
 h₁' : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_bicat_ver_id_comp
       ⟦ w, x ⟧)
(h₂ : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_bicat_ver_id_comp
      ⟦ y, z ⟧)
(v₁ : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
        double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_bicat_ver_id_comp
      ⟦ w, y ⟧)
(v₂ : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
        double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_bicat_ver_id_comp
      ⟦ x, z ⟧),
h₁ ==> h₁'
→ square_double_bicat h₁' h₂ v₁ v₂
  → square_double_bicat h₁ h₂ v₁ v₂
 exact (λ (w x y z : C)
               (v₁ v₁' : w -->v x) (v₂ : y -->v z)
               (h₁ : w -->h y) (h₂ : x -->h z)
               (p : v₁ = v₁')
               (s : square v₁' v₂ h₁ h₂),
             transportf_square
               (!p)
               (idpath _)
               s).
    
C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
∏
(w x y
 z : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_bicat_ver_id_comp)

  → square_double_bicat h₁ h₂' v₁ v₂
 exact (λ (w x y z : C)
               (v₁ : w -->v x) (v₂ v₂' : y -->v z)

               (p : v₂ = v₂')

             transportf_square
               (idpath _)
               p
               s).
  Defined.

(w x y z : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker)

(v₁ v₁'
 v₁'' : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
          double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
        ⟦ w, y ⟧)
(v₂ : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
        double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
      ⟦ x, z ⟧) (τ₁ : v₁ ==> v₁') (τ₂ : v₁' ==> v₁'')
(s : square_double_bicat h₁ h₂ v₁'' v₂),
lwhisker_square (τ₁ • τ₂) s =
lwhisker_square τ₁ (lwhisker_square τ₂ s)
 
C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
w, x, y, z: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
v₁: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ w, x
⟧
v₂: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ y, z
⟧
h₁, h₁', h₁'': ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
  double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
⟦ w, y ⟧
h₂: ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
  double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ x,
z ⟧
s₁: h₁ ==> h₁'
s₂: h₁' ==> h₁''
s₃: square_double_bicat v₁ v₂ h₁'' h₂
lwhisker_square (s₁ • s₂) s₃ =
lwhisker_square s₁ (lwhisker_square s₂ s₃)

      
C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
w, x, y, z: C
v₁: C ⟦ w, x ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
h₁, h₁', h₁'': w -->h y
h₂: x -->h z
s₁: square (identity_v w) (identity_v y) h₁ h₁'
s₂: square (identity_v w) (identity_v y) h₁' h₁''
s₃: square v₁ v₂ h₁'' h₂
transportf_square (id_v_left v₁) (id_v_left v₂)
  (transportf_square (id_v_left (identity_v w))
     (id_v_left (identity_v y)) (s₁ ⋆v s₂) ⋆v s₃) =
transportf_square (id_v_left v₁) (id_v_left v₂)
  (s₁
   ⋆v transportf_square (id_v_left v₁) (id_v_left v₂)
        (s₂ ⋆v s₃))

      
C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
w, x, y, z: C
v₁: C ⟦ w, x ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
h₁, h₁', h₁'': w -->h y
h₂: x -->h z
s₁: square (identity_v w) (identity_v y) h₁ h₁'
s₂: square (identity_v w) (identity_v y) h₁' h₁''
s₃: square v₁ v₂ h₁'' h₂
transportf_square (id_v_left v₁) (id_v_left v₂)
  (transportf_square
     (maponpaths (λ z : w -->v w, z ·v v₁)
        (id_v_left (identity_v w)))
     (maponpaths (λ z0 : y -->v y, z0 ·v v₂)
        (id_v_left (identity_v y))) (s₁ ⋆v s₂ ⋆v s₃)) =
transportf_square (id_v_left v₁) (id_v_left v₂)
  (s₁
   ⋆v transportf_square (id_v_left v₁) (id_v_left v₂)
        (s₂ ⋆v s₃))

      
C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
w, x, y, z: C
v₁: C ⟦ w, x ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
h₁, h₁', h₁'': w -->h y
h₂: x -->h z
s₁: square (identity_v w) (identity_v y) h₁ h₁'
s₂: square (identity_v w) (identity_v y) h₁' h₁''
s₃: square v₁ v₂ h₁'' h₂
transportf_square (id_v_left v₁) (id_v_left v₂)
  (transportf_square
     (maponpaths (λ z : w -->v w, z ·v v₁)
        (id_v_left (identity_v w)))
     (maponpaths (λ z0 : y -->v y, z0 ·v v₂)
        (id_v_left (identity_v y))) (s₁ ⋆v s₂ ⋆v s₃)) =
transportf_square (id_v_left v₁) (id_v_left v₂)
  (transportf_square
     (maponpaths (λ z : w -->v x, identity_v w ·v z)
        (id_v_left v₁))
     (maponpaths (λ z0 : y -->v z, identity_v y ·v z0)
        (id_v_left v₂)) (s₁ ⋆v (s₂ ⋆v s₃)))

      
C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
w, x, y, z: C
v₁: C ⟦ w, x ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
h₁, h₁', h₁'': w -->h y
h₂: x -->h z
s₁: square (identity_v w) (identity_v y) h₁ h₁'
s₂: square (identity_v w) (identity_v y) h₁' h₁''
s₃: square v₁ v₂ h₁'' h₂
transportf_square (id_v_left v₁) (id_v_left v₂)
  (transportf_square
     (maponpaths (λ z : w -->v x, identity_v w ·v z)
        (id_v_left v₁))
     (maponpaths (λ z0 : y -->v z, identity_v y ·v z0)
        (id_v_left v₂)) (s₁ ⋆v (s₂ ⋆v s₃))) =
transportf_square (id_v_left v₁) (id_v_left v₂)
  (transportf_square
     (maponpaths (λ z : w -->v w, z ·v v₁)
        (id_v_left (identity_v w)))
     (maponpaths (λ z0 : y -->v y, z0 ·v v₂)
        (id_v_left (identity_v y))) (s₁ ⋆v s₂ ⋆v s₃))

C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
w, x, y, z: C
v₁: C ⟦ w, x ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
h₁, h₁', h₁'': w -->h y
h₂: x -->h z

s₃: square v₁ v₂ h₁'' h₂
transportf_square (id_v_left v₁) (id_v_left v₂)
  (transportf_square
     (maponpaths (λ z : w -->v x, identity_v w ·v z)
        (id_v_left v₁))
     (maponpaths (λ z0 : y -->v z, identity_v y ·v z0)
        (id_v_left v₂))
     (transportf_square
        (! assoc (identity_v w) (identity_v w) v₁)
        (! assoc (identity_v y) (identity_v y) v₂)
        (s₁ ⋆v s₂ ⋆v s₃))) =
transportf_square (id_v_left v₁) (id_v_left v₂)
  (transportf_square
     (maponpaths (λ z : w -->v w, z ·v v₁)
        (id_v_left (identity_v w)))
     (maponpaths (λ z0 : y -->v y, z0 ·v v₂)

C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
w, x, y, z: C
v₁: C ⟦ w, x ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
h₁, h₁', h₁'': w -->h y
h₂: x -->h z
s₁: square (identity_v w) (identity_v y) h₁ h₁'
s₂: square (identity_v w) (identity_v y) h₁' h₁''
s₃: square v₁ v₂ h₁'' h₂
transportf_square
  (! assoc (identity_v w) (identity_v w) v₁ @
   maponpaths (λ z : w -->v x, identity_v w ·v z)
     (id_v_left v₁) @ id_v_left v₁)
  (! assoc (identity_v y) (identity_v y) v₂ @
   maponpaths (λ z0 : y -->v z, identity_v y ·v z0)
     (id_v_left v₂) @ id_v_left v₂) (s₁ ⋆v s₂ ⋆v s₃) =
transportf_square
  (maponpaths (λ z : w -->v w, z ·v v₁)
     (id_v_left (identity_v w)) @ id_v_left v₁)
  (maponpaths (λ z0 : y -->v y, z0 ·v v₂)
     (id_v_left (identity_v y)) @ id_v_left v₂)
  (s₁ ⋆v s₂ ⋆v s₃)

ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
∏
(w x y z : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker)
(h₁ : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ w,
      x ⟧)

      z ⟧)

        double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
      ⟦ w, y ⟧)
(v₂ v₂'
 v₂'' : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
          double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
        ⟦ x, z ⟧) (τ₁ : v₂ ==> v₂')
(τ₂ : v₂' ==> v₂'')
(s : square_double_bicat h₁ h₂ v₁ v₂),
rwhisker_square (τ₁ • τ₂) s =
rwhisker_square τ₂ (rwhisker_square τ₁ s)
 
C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
w, x, y, z: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
v₁: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ w, x
⟧
v₂: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ y, z
⟧
h₁: ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
  double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ w,
y ⟧
h₂, h₂', h₂'': ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
  double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
⟦ x, z ⟧
s₁: h₂ ==> h₂'
s₂: h₂' ==> h₂''
s₃: square_double_bicat v₁ v₂ h₁ h₂
rwhisker_square (s₁ • s₂) s₃ =
rwhisker_square s₂ (rwhisker_square s₁ s₃)

     (maponpaths (λ z : x -->v x, v₁ ·v z)
        (id_v_left (identity_v x)))
     (maponpaths (λ z0 : z -->v z, v₂ ·v z0)
        (id_v_left (identity_v z)))
     (transportf_square
        (! assoc v₁ (identity_v x) (identity_v x))
        (! assoc v₂ (identity_v z) (identity_v z))
        (s₃ ⋆v s₁ ⋆v s₂))) =
transportf_square (id_v_right v₁) (id_v_right v₂)
  (transportf_square
     (maponpaths (λ z : w -->v x, z ·v identity_v x)
        (id_v_right v₁))
     (maponpaths (λ z0 : y -->v z, z0 ·v identity_v z)
        (id_v_right v₂)) (s₃ ⋆v s₁ ⋆v s₂))

      
C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
w, x, y, z: C
v₁: C ⟦ w, x ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
h₁: w -->h y
h₂, h₂', h₂'': x -->h z
s₁: square (identity_v x) (identity_v z) h₂ h₂'
s₂: square (identity_v x) (identity_v z) h₂' h₂''
s₃: square v₁ v₂ h₁ h₂
transportf_square
  (! assoc v₁ (identity_v x) (identity_v x) @
   maponpaths (λ z : x -->v x, v₁ ·v z)
     (id_v_left (identity_v x)) @ id_v_right v₁)
  (! assoc v₂ (identity_v z) (identity_v z) @
   maponpaths (λ z0 : z -->v z, v₂ ·v z0)
     (id_v_left (identity_v z)) @ id_v_right v₂)
  (s₃ ⋆v s₁ ⋆v s₂) =
transportf_square
  (maponpaths (λ z : w -->v x, z ·v identity_v x)
     (id_v_right v₁) @ id_v_right v₁)
  (maponpaths (λ z0 : y -->v z, z0 ·v identity_v z)
     (id_v_right v₂) @ id_v_right v₂) (s₃ ⋆v s₁ ⋆v s₂)

      
C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat

h₁: w -->h y

s₁: square (identity_v x) (identity_v z) h₂ h₂'
s₂: square (identity_v x) (identity_v z) h₂' h₂''
s₃: square v₁ v₂ h₁ h₂
s₃ ⋆v s₁ ⋆v s₂ = s₃ ⋆v s₁ ⋆v s₂

      apply idpath.

C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
w, x, y, z: C
v₁: C ⟦ w, x ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
h₁, h₁': w -->h y
h₂, h₂': x -->h z
s₁: square (identity_v w) (identity_v y) h₁ h₁'

s₃: square v₁ v₂ h₁' h₂
transportf_square (id_v_left v₁) (id_v_left v₂)
  (transportf_square
     (maponpaths (λ z : w -->v x, identity_v w ·v z)
        (id_v_right v₁))
     (maponpaths (λ z0 : y -->v z, identity_v y ·v z0)
        (id_v_right v₂))
     (transportb_square
        (assoc (identity_v w) v₁ (identity_v x))
        (assoc (identity_v y) v₂ (identity_v z))
        (s₁ ⋆v s₃ ⋆v s₂))) =

  (transportf_square
     (maponpaths (λ z : w -->v x, z ·v identity_v x)
        (id_v_left v₁))
     (maponpaths (λ z0 : y -->v z, z0 ·v identity_v z)
        (id_v_left v₂)) (s₁ ⋆v s₃ ⋆v s₂))

      
C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
w, x, y, z: C
v₁: C ⟦ w, x ⟧

h₂, h₂': x -->h z

transportf_square (id_v_left v₁) (id_v_left v₂)
  (transportf_square
     (maponpaths (λ z : w -->v x, identity_v w ·v z)
        (id_v_right v₁))
     (maponpaths (λ z0 : y -->v z, identity_v y ·v z0)

        (! assoc (identity_v w) v₁ (identity_v x))
        (! assoc (identity_v y) v₂ (identity_v z))
        (s₁ ⋆v s₃ ⋆v s₂))) =

  (transportf_square
     (maponpaths (λ z : w -->v x, z ·v identity_v x)
        (id_v_left v₁))
     (maponpaths (λ z0 : y -->v z, z0 ·v identity_v z)
        (id_v_left v₂)) (s₁ ⋆v s₃ ⋆v s₂))

      
C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
w, x, y, z: C
v₁: C ⟦ w, x ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
h₁, h₁': w -->h y
h₂, h₂': x -->h z
s₁: square (identity_v w) (identity_v y) h₁ h₁'
s₂: square (identity_v x) (identity_v z) h₂ h₂'
s₃: square v₁ v₂ h₁' h₂
transportf_square
  (! assoc (identity_v w) v₁ (identity_v x) @
   maponpaths (λ z : w -->v x, identity_v w ·v z)
     (id_v_right v₁) @ id_v_left v₁)
  (! assoc (identity_v y) v₂ (identity_v z) @
   maponpaths (λ z0 : y -->v z, identity_v y ·v z0)
     (id_v_right v₂) @ id_v_left v₂) (s₁ ⋆v s₃ ⋆v s₂) =
transportf_square
  (maponpaths (λ z : w -->v x, z ·v identity_v x)
     (id_v_left v₁) @ id_v_right v₁)
  (maponpaths (λ z0 : y -->v z, z0 ·v identity_v z)
     (id_v_left v₂) @ id_v_right v₂) (s₁ ⋆v s₃ ⋆v s₂)

      
C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
w, x, y, z: C
v₁: C ⟦ w, x ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
h₁, h₁': w -->h y
h₂, h₂': x -->h z
s₁: square (identity_v w) (identity_v y) h₁ h₁'
s₂: square (identity_v x) (identity_v z) h₂ h₂'
s₃: square v₁ v₂ h₁' h₂
s₁ ⋆v s₃ ⋆v s₂ = s₁ ⋆v s₃ ⋆v s₂

      apply idpath.

 y₃ : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker)
(h₁ : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ x₁,
      x₂ ⟧)
(h₂ : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ x₂,
      x₃ ⟧)
(k₁ : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ y₁,
      y₂ ⟧)
(k₂ : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ y₂,
      y₃ ⟧)
(v₁
 v₁' : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
         double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
       ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧)
(v₂ : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
        double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
      ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧)
(v₃ : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
        double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
      ⟦ x₃, y₃ ⟧) (τ : v₁ ==> v₁')
(s₁ : square_double_bicat h₁ k₁ v₁' v₂)
(s₂ : square_double_bicat h₂ k₂ v₂ v₃),
lwhisker_square τ (comp_h_square_bicat s₁ s₂) =
comp_h_square_bicat (lwhisker_square τ s₁) s₂
 
C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
x₁, x₂, x₃, y₁, y₂, y₃: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
v₁: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ x₁,
x₂ ⟧
v₂: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ x₂,
x₃ ⟧
w₁: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ y₁,
y₂ ⟧
w₂: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ y₂,
y₃ ⟧
h₁, h₁': ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧
h₂: ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
  double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧
h₃: ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
  double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
⟦ x₃, y₃ ⟧
s₁: h₁ ==> h₁'
s₂: square_double_bicat v₁ w₁ h₁' h₂
s₃: square_double_bicat v₂ w₂ h₂ h₃
lwhisker_square s₁ (comp_h_square_bicat s₂ s₃) =
comp_h_square_bicat (lwhisker_square s₁ s₂) s₃

      
C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
x₁, x₂, x₃, y₁, y₂, y₃: C
v₁: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
w₁: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
w₂: C ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧
h₁, h₁': x₁ -->h y₁
h₂: x₂ -->h y₂
h₃: x₃ -->h y₃
s₁: square (identity_v x₁) (identity_v y₁) h₁ h₁'
s₂: square v₁ w₁ h₁' h₂
s₃: square v₂ w₂ h₂ h₃
transportf_square (id_v_left (v₁ · v₂))
  (id_v_left (w₁ · w₂)) (s₁ ⋆v (s₂ ⋆v s₃)) =
transportf_square (id_v_left v₁) (id_v_left w₁)
  (s₁ ⋆v s₂) ⋆v s₃

  (! assoc (identity_v x₁) v₁ v₂ @ id_v_left (v₁ · v₂))
  (! assoc (identity_v y₁) w₁ w₂ @ id_v_left (w₁ · w₂))
  (s₁ ⋆v s₂ ⋆v s₃) =

  (maponpaths (λ z : x₁ -->v x₂, z ·v v₂)

∏
(x₁ x₂ x₃ y₁ y₂
 y₃ : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker)
(h₁ : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ x₁,
      x₂ ⟧)
(h₂ : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ x₂,
      x₃ ⟧)
(k₁ : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ y₁,
      y₂ ⟧)
(k₂ : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ y₂,
      y₃ ⟧)
(v₁ : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
        double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
      ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧)
(v₂ : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
        double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
      ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧)
(v₃
 v₃' : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
         double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
       ⟦ x₃, y₃ ⟧) (τ : v₃ ==> v₃')
(s₁ : square_double_bicat h₁ k₁ v₁ v₂)
(s₂ : square_double_bicat h₂ k₂ v₂ v₃),
rwhisker_square τ (comp_h_square_bicat s₁ s₂) =
comp_h_square_bicat s₁ (rwhisker_square τ s₂)
 
C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
x₁, x₂, x₃, y₁, y₂, y₃: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
v₁: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ x₁,
x₂ ⟧
v₂: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ x₂,
x₃ ⟧
w₁: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ y₁,
y₂ ⟧
w₂: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ y₂,
y₃ ⟧
h₁: ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
  double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧
h₂: ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
  double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧
h₃, h₃': ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
⟦ x₃, y₃ ⟧
s₁: h₃ ==> h₃'
s₂: square_double_bicat v₁ w₁ h₁ h₂
s₃: square_double_bicat v₂ w₂ h₂ h₃
rwhisker_square s₁ (comp_h_square_bicat s₂ s₃) =
comp_h_square_bicat s₂ (rwhisker_square s₁ s₃)

      
C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
x₁, x₂, x₃, y₁, y₂, y₃: C
v₁: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
w₁: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
w₂: C ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧
h₁: x₁ -->h y₁
h₂: x₂ -->h y₂
h₃, h₃': x₃ -->h y₃
s₁: square (identity_v x₃) (identity_v y₃) h₃ h₃'
s₂: square v₁ w₁ h₁ h₂
s₃: square v₂ w₂ h₂ h₃
transportf_square (id_v_right (v₁ · v₂))
  (id_v_right (w₁ · w₂)) (s₂ ⋆v s₃ ⋆v s₁) =
s₂
⋆v transportf_square (id_v_right v₂) (id_v_right w₂)
     (s₃ ⋆v s₁)

s₂: square v₁ w₁ h₁ h₂
s₃: square v₂ w₂ h₂ h₃
s₂ ⋆v (s₃ ⋆v s₁) = ?t2

        apply square_assoc_v.
      
C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
x₁, x₂, x₃, y₁, y₂, y₃: C
v₁: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧
w₁: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
w₂: C ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧
h₁: x₁ -->h y₁
h₂: x₂ -->h y₂
h₃, h₃': x₃ -->h y₃
s₁: square (identity_v x₃) (identity_v y₃) h₃ h₃'
s₂: square v₁ w₁ h₁ h₂
s₃: square v₂ w₂ h₂ h₃
transportf_square
  (maponpaths (λ z : x₂ -->v x₃, v₁ ·v z)
     (id_v_right v₂))
  (maponpaths (λ z : y₂ -->v y₃, w₁ ·v z)
     (id_v_right w₂))
  (transportb_square (assoc v₁ v₂ (identity_v x₃))
     (assoc w₁ w₂ (identity_v y₃)) (s₂ ⋆v s₃ ⋆v s₁)) =
transportf_square (id_v_right (v₁ · v₂))
  (id_v_right (w₁ · w₂)) (s₂ ⋆v s₃ ⋆v s₁)

C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
∏ (x y z : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker)
(h : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
       double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ x,
     y ⟧)
(k : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
       double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ y,
     z ⟧),
comp_v_square_bicat (id_h_square_bicat h)
  (id_h_square_bicat k) = id_h_square_bicat (h · k)

     ⟧)
(w : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ y, z
     ⟧),
comp_h_square_bicat (id_v_square_bicat v)
  (id_v_square_bicat w) = id_v_square_bicat (v · w)

∏
(w₁ w₂ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ z₁
 z₂ : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker)
(hw : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ w₁,
      w₂ ⟧)
(hx : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ x₁,
      x₂ ⟧)
(hy : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ y₁,
      y₂ ⟧)
(hz : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ z₁,
      z₂ ⟧)
(u₁ : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
        double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
      ⟦ w₁, x₁ ⟧)
(u₂ : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
        double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
      ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧)
(u₃ : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
        double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
      ⟦ y₁, z₁ ⟧)
(v₁ : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
        double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
      ⟦ w₂, x₂ ⟧)
(v₂ : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
        double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
      ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧)
(v₃ : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
        double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
      ⟦ y₂, z₂ ⟧)
(s₁ : square_double_bicat hw hx u₁ v₁)
(s₂ : square_double_bicat hx hy u₂ v₂)
(s₃ : square_double_bicat hy hz u₃ v₃),
is_ver_cylinder
  (comp_v_square_bicat s₁ (comp_v_square_bicat s₂ s₃))
  (comp_v_square_bicat (comp_v_square_bicat s₁ s₂) s₃)
  (lassociator u₁ u₂ u₃) (lassociator v₁ v₂ v₃)

ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
w₁, w₂, x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂, z₁, z₂: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
hw: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ w₁,
w₂ ⟧
hx: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ x₁,

z₂ ⟧
u₁: ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
  double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker

  double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker

  double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker

s₁: square_double_bicat hw hx u₁ v₁
s₂: square_double_bicat hx hy u₂ v₂
s₃: square_double_bicat hy hz u₃ v₃
transportf_square (id_v_left hw) (id_v_left hz)
  (lassociator_h u₁ u₂ u₃ ⋆v s₁ ⋆h s₂ ⋆h s₃) =
transportf_square (id_v_right hw) (id_v_right hz)
  (s₁ ⋆h (s₂ ⋆h s₃) ⋆v lassociator_h v₁ v₂ v₃)

(x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ z₁
 z₂ : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker)

      x₂ ⟧)

      y₂ ⟧)

(v₁
 v₁' : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
         double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
       ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧)
(v₂
 v₂' : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
         double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
       ⟦ y₁, z₁ ⟧)

 w₁' : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
         double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
       ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧)
(w₂
 w₂' : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
         double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
       ⟦ y₂, z₂ ⟧) (τ₁ : v₁ ==> v₁') (τ₂ : v₂ ==> v₂')
(θ₁ : w₁ ==> w₁') (θ₂ : w₂ ==> w₂')
(s₁ : square_double_bicat h₁ h₂ v₁ w₁)
(s₁' : square_double_bicat h₁ h₂ v₁' w₁')
(s₂ : square_double_bicat h₂ h₃ v₂ w₂)
(s₂' : square_double_bicat h₂ h₃ v₂' w₂'),
is_ver_cylinder s₁ s₁' τ₁ θ₁
→ is_ver_cylinder s₂ s₂' τ₂ θ₂
  → is_ver_cylinder (comp_v_square_bicat s₁ s₂)
      (comp_v_square_bicat s₁' s₂') (τ₂ ⋆⋆ τ₁)
      (θ₂ ⋆⋆ θ₁)

v₂: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧

s₁': square (identity_v y₁) (identity_v z₁) h₂ h₂'

s₂': square (identity_v y₂) (identity_v z₂) k₂ k₂'
s₃: square v₁ v₂ h₁ k₁
s₃': square v₁ v₂ h₁' k₁'
s₄: square v₂ v₃ h₂ k₂
s₄': square v₂ v₃ h₂' k₂'
p: transportf_square (id_v_left v₁) (id_v_left v₂)
  (s₁ ⋆v s₃') =
transportf_square (id_v_right v₁) (id_v_right v₂)
  (s₃ ⋆v s₂)
q: transportf_square (id_v_left v₂) (id_v_left v₃)
  (s₁' ⋆v s₄') =
transportf_square (id_v_right v₂) (id_v_right v₃)
  (s₄ ⋆v s₂')

  (transportf_square (id_v_left (identity_v x₁))
     (id_v_left (identity_v z₁))
     (s₁ ⋆h id_v_square h₂ ⋆v id_v_square h₁' ⋆h s₁')
   ⋆v s₃' ⋆h s₄') =

  (s₃ ⋆h s₄
   ⋆v transportf_square (id_v_left (identity_v x₂))
        (id_v_left (identity_v z₂))
        (s₂ ⋆h id_v_square k₂
         ⋆v id_v_square k₁' ⋆h s₂'))

h₁, h₁': x₁ -->h y₁

k₁, k₁': x₂ -->h y₂
k₂, k₂': y₂ -->h z₂
s₁: square (identity_v x₁) (identity_v y₁) h₁ h₁'
s₁': square (identity_v y₁) (identity_v z₁) h₂ h₂'
s₂: square (identity_v x₂) (identity_v y₂) k₁ k₁'
s₂': square (identity_v y₂) (identity_v z₂) k₂ k₂'
s₃: square v₁ v₂ h₁ k₁
s₃': square v₁ v₂ h₁' k₁'
s₄: square v₂ v₃ h₂ k₂
s₄': square v₂ v₃ h₂' k₂'
p: transportf_square (id_v_left v₁) (id_v_left v₂)
  (s₁ ⋆v s₃') =
transportf_square (id_v_right v₁) (id_v_right v₂)
  (s₃ ⋆v s₂)
q: transportf_square (id_v_left v₂) (id_v_left v₃)
  (s₁' ⋆v s₄') =
transportf_square (id_v_right v₂) (id_v_right v₃)
  (s₄ ⋆v s₂')
p': s₁ ⋆v s₃' =
transportf_square (! id_v_left v₁)
  (! id_v_left v₂)
  (transportf_square (id_v_right v₁)
     (id_v_right v₂) (s₃ ⋆v s₂))
transportf_square (id_v_left v₁) (id_v_left v₃)
  (transportf_square (id_v_left (identity_v x₁))
     (id_v_left (identity_v z₁))
     (s₁ ⋆h id_v_square h₂ ⋆v id_v_square h₁' ⋆h s₁')
   ⋆v s₃' ⋆h s₄') =
transportf_square (id_v_right v₁) (id_v_right v₃)
  (s₃ ⋆h s₄
   ⋆v transportf_square (id_v_left (identity_v x₂))
        (id_v_left (identity_v z₂))
        (s₂ ⋆h id_v_square k₂
         ⋆v id_v_square k₁' ⋆h s₂'))

      
C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂, z₁, z₂: C
v₁: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
v₃: C ⟦ z₁, z₂ ⟧
h₁, h₁': x₁ -->h y₁
h₂, h₂': y₁ -->h z₁
k₁, k₁': x₂ -->h y₂
k₂, k₂': y₂ -->h z₂
s₁: square (identity_v x₁) (identity_v y₁) h₁ h₁'
s₁': square (identity_v y₁) (identity_v z₁) h₂ h₂'

s₂': square (identity_v y₂) (identity_v z₂) k₂ k₂'

s₄': square v₂ v₃ h₂' k₂'

  (s₁ ⋆v s₃') =
transportf_square (id_v_right v₁) (id_v_right v₂)
  (s₃ ⋆v s₂)

  (s₁' ⋆v s₄') =
transportf_square (id_v_right v₂) (id_v_right v₃)
  (s₄ ⋆v s₂')
p': s₁ ⋆v s₃' =
transportf_square
  (id_v_right v₁ @ ! id_v_left v₁)
  (id_v_right v₂ @ ! id_v_left v₂) (s₃ ⋆v s₂)
transportf_square (id_v_left v₁) (id_v_left v₃)
  (transportf_square (id_v_left (identity_v x₁))
     (id_v_left (identity_v z₁))
     (s₁ ⋆h id_v_square h₂ ⋆v id_v_square h₁' ⋆h s₁')
   ⋆v s₃' ⋆h s₄') =
transportf_square (id_v_right v₁) (id_v_right v₃)

   ⋆v transportf_square (id_v_left (identity_v x₂))
        (id_v_left (identity_v z₂))
        (s₂ ⋆h id_v_square k₂
         ⋆v id_v_square k₁' ⋆h s₂'))

v₂: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧

h₁, h₁': x₁ -->h y₁
h₂, h₂': y₁ -->h z₁

s₁': square (identity_v y₁) (identity_v z₁) h₂ h₂'
s₂: square (identity_v x₂) (identity_v y₂) k₁ k₁'
s₂': square (identity_v y₂) (identity_v z₂) k₂ k₂'

q': s₁' ⋆v s₄' =
transportf_square
  (id_v_right v₂ @ ! id_v_left v₂)
  (id_v_right v₃ @ ! id_v_left v₃) (s₄ ⋆v s₂')
transportf_square (id_v_left v₁) (id_v_left v₃)
  (transportf_square
     (maponpaths (λ z : x₁ -->v x₁, z ·v v₁)
        (id_v_left (identity_v x₁)))
     (maponpaths (λ z : z₁ -->v z₁, z ·v v₃)
        (id_v_left (identity_v z₁)))
     (s₁ ⋆h id_v_square h₂ ⋆v id_v_square h₁' ⋆h s₁'
      ⋆v s₃' ⋆h s₄')) =
transportf_square (id_v_right v₁) (id_v_right v₃)

q': s₁' ⋆v s₄' =
transportf_square
  (id_v_right v₂ @ ! id_v_left v₂)
  (id_v_right v₃ @ ! id_v_left v₃) (s₄ ⋆v s₂')
transportf_square (id_v_left v₁) (id_v_left v₃)
  (transportf_square
     (maponpaths (λ z : x₁ -->v x₁, z ·v v₁)
        (id_v_left (identity_v x₁)))
     (maponpaths (λ z : z₁ -->v z₁, z ·v v₃)
        (id_v_left (identity_v z₁)))
     (s₁ ⋆h id_v_square h₂ ⋆v id_v_square h₁' ⋆h s₁'
      ⋆v s₃' ⋆h s₄')) =
transportf_square (id_v_right v₁) (id_v_right v₃)
  (transportf_square
     (maponpaths (λ z : x₂ -->v x₂, v₁ ·v z)
        (id_v_left (identity_v x₂)))
     (maponpaths (λ z : z₂ -->v z₂, v₃ ·v z)
        (id_v_left (identity_v z₂)))
     (s₃ ⋆h s₄
      ⋆v (s₂ ⋆h id_v_square k₂
          ⋆v id_v_square k₁' ⋆h s₂')))

      
C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂, z₁, z₂: C

s₂': square (identity_v y₂) (identity_v z₂) k₂ k₂'
s₃: square v₁ v₂ h₁ k₁
s₃': square v₁ v₂ h₁' k₁'
s₄: square v₂ v₃ h₂ k₂
s₄': square v₂ v₃ h₂' k₂'

  (id_v_right v₂ @ ! id_v_left v₂) (s₃ ⋆v s₂)

  (id_v_right v₂ @ ! id_v_left v₂)
  (id_v_right v₃ @ ! id_v_left v₃) (s₄ ⋆v s₂')
transportf_square
  (maponpaths (λ z : x₁ -->v x₁, z ·v v₁)
     (id_v_left (identity_v x₁)) @ id_v_left v₁)
  (maponpaths (λ z : z₁ -->v z₁, z ·v v₃)
     (id_v_left (identity_v z₁)) @ id_v_left v₃)
  (s₁ ⋆h id_v_square h₂ ⋆v id_v_square h₁' ⋆h s₁'
   ⋆v s₃' ⋆h s₄') =
transportf_square
  (maponpaths (λ z : x₂ -->v x₂, v₁ ·v z)
     (id_v_left (identity_v x₂)) @ id_v_right v₁)
  (maponpaths (λ z : z₂ -->v z₂, v₃ ·v z)
     (id_v_left (identity_v z₂)) @ id_v_right v₃)
  (s₃ ⋆h s₄
   ⋆v (s₂ ⋆h id_v_square k₂ ⋆v id_v_square k₁' ⋆h s₂'))

        (id_v_right v₂ @ ! id_v_left v₂) (s₃ ⋆v s₂))
   ⋆h transportf_square
        (maponpaths (λ z : y₁ -->v y₁, z ·v v₂)
           (! id_left (identity_v y₁)))
        (maponpaths (λ z : z₁ -->v z₁, z ·v v₃)
           (! id_left (identity_v z₁)))
        (transportf_square
           (id_v_right v₂ @ ! id_v_left v₂)
           (id_v_right v₃ @ ! id_v_left v₃)
           (s₄ ⋆v s₂'))) =
transportf_square
  (maponpaths (λ z : x₂ -->v x₂, v₁ ·v z)
     (id_v_left (identity_v x₂)) @ id_v_right v₁)
  (maponpaths (λ z : z₂ -->v z₂, v₃ ·v z)
     (id_v_left (identity_v z₂)) @ id_v_right v₃)
  (transportf_square
     (maponpaths (λ z : x₂ -->v x₂, v₁ ·v z)
        (! id_right (identity_v x₂)))
     (maponpaths (λ z : y₂ -->v y₂, v₂ ·v z)
        (! id_right (identity_v y₂))) (s₃ ⋆v s₂)
   ⋆h transportf_square
        (maponpaths (λ z : y₂ -->v y₂, v₂ ·v z)
           (! id_left (identity_v y₂)))
        (maponpaths (λ z : z₂ -->v z₂, v₃ ·v z)
           (! id_left (identity_v z₂))) (s₄ ⋆v s₂'))

  (((id_v_right v₁ @ ! id_v_left v₁) @
    maponpaths (λ z : x₁ -->v x₁, z ·v v₁)
      (! id_right (identity_v x₁))) @
   maponpaths (λ z : x₁ -->v x₁, z ·v v₁)
     (id_v_left (identity_v x₁)) @ id_v_left v₁)
  (maponpaths (λ z : z₁ -->v z₁, z ·v v₃)
     (id_v_left (identity_v z₁)) @ id_v_left v₃)
  (transportf_square (idpath (v₁ ·v identity_v x₂))
     (((id_v_right v₃ @ ! id_v_left v₃) @
       maponpaths (λ z : z₁ -->v z₁, z ·v v₃)
         (! id_left (identity_v z₁))) @
      idpath (identity_v z₁ · identity_v z₁ ·v v₃))
     (transportf_square (idpath (v₁ ·v identity_v x₂))
        (! (((id_v_right v₂ @ ! id_v_left v₂) @
             maponpaths (λ z : y₁ -->v y₁, z ·v v₂)
               (! id_left (identity_v y₁))) @
            ! ((id_v_right v₂ @ ! id_v_left v₂) @
               maponpaths (λ z : y₁ -->v y₁, z ·v v₂)
                 (! id_right (identity_v y₁)))))
        (s₃ ⋆v s₂) ⋆h (s₄ ⋆v s₂'))) = ?b

k₂, k₂': y₂ -->h z₂
s₁: square (identity_v x₁) (identity_v y₁) h₁ h₁'
s₁': square (identity_v y₁) (identity_v z₁) h₂ h₂'
s₂: square (identity_v x₂) (identity_v y₂) k₁ k₁'
s₂': square (identity_v y₂) (identity_v z₂) k₂ k₂'
s₃: square v₁ v₂ h₁ k₁
s₃': square v₁ v₂ h₁' k₁'
s₄: square v₂ v₃ h₂ k₂
s₄': square v₂ v₃ h₂' k₂'
p': s₁ ⋆v s₃' =
transportf_square
  (id_v_right v₁ @ ! id_v_left v₁)
  (id_v_right v₂ @ ! id_v_left v₂) (s₃ ⋆v s₂)
q': s₁' ⋆v s₄' =
transportf_square
  (id_v_right v₂ @ ! id_v_left v₂)
  (id_v_right v₃ @ ! id_v_left v₃) (s₄ ⋆v s₂')
transportf_square
  (maponpaths (λ z : x₂ -->v x₂, v₁ ·v z)
     (id_v_left (identity_v x₂)) @ id_v_right v₁)
  (maponpaths (λ z : z₂ -->v z₂, v₃ ·v z)
     (id_v_left (identity_v z₂)) @ id_v_right v₃)
  (transportf_square
     (maponpaths (λ z : x₂ -->v x₂, v₁ ·v z)
        (! id_right (identity_v x₂)))
     (idpath (v₃ ·v identity_v z₂ · identity_v z₂))
     ((s₃ ⋆v s₂)
      ⋆h transportf_square
           (! maponpaths (λ z : y₂ -->v y₂, v₂ ·v z)
                (! id_right (identity_v y₂)))
           (idpath
              (v₃ ·v identity_v z₂ · identity_v z₂))
           (transportf_square
              (maponpaths (λ z : y₂ -->v y₂, v₂ ·v z)
                 (! id_left (identity_v y₂)))
              (maponpaths (λ z : z₂ -->v z₂, v₃ ·v z)
                 (! id_left (identity_v z₂)))
              (s₄ ⋆v s₂')))) = ?b

transportf_square
  (id_v_right v₂ @ ! id_v_left v₂)
  (id_v_right v₃ @ ! id_v_left v₃) (s₄ ⋆v s₂')
transportf_square
  (maponpaths (λ z : x₂ -->v x₂, v₁ ·v z)
     (! id_right (identity_v x₂)) @
   maponpaths (λ z : x₂ -->v x₂, v₁ ·v z)
     (id_v_left (identity_v x₂)) @ id_v_right v₁)
  (idpath (v₃ ·v identity_v z₂ · identity_v z₂) @
   maponpaths (λ z : z₂ -->v z₂, v₃ ·v z)
     (id_v_left (identity_v z₂)) @ id_v_right v₃)
  ((s₃ ⋆v s₂)
   ⋆h transportf_square
        (maponpaths (λ z : y₂ -->v y₂, v₂ ·v z)
           (! id_left (identity_v y₂)) @
         ! maponpaths (λ z : y₂ -->v y₂, v₂ ·v z)
             (! id_right (identity_v y₂)))
        (maponpaths (λ z : z₂ -->v z₂, v₃ ·v z)
           (! id_left (identity_v z₂)) @
         idpath (v₃ ·v identity_v z₂ · identity_v z₂))
        (s₄ ⋆v s₂')) = ?b

      idpath (v₃ ·v identity_v z₂ · identity_v z₂))

              (! id_left (identity_v y₂)) @
            ! maponpaths (λ z : y₂ -->v y₂, v₂ ·v z)
                (! id_right (identity_v y₂))))
        (s₃ ⋆v s₂) ⋆h (s₄ ⋆v s₂'))) = ?b

C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂, z₁, z₂: C
v₁: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
v₂: C ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧
v₃: C ⟦ z₁, z₂ ⟧
h₁, h₁': x₁ -->h y₁
h₂, h₂': y₁ -->h z₁
k₁, k₁': x₂ -->h y₂
k₂, k₂': y₂ -->h z₂
s₁: square (identity_v x₁) (identity_v y₁) h₁ h₁'
s₁': square (identity_v y₁) (identity_v z₁) h₂ h₂'
s₂: square (identity_v x₂) (identity_v y₂) k₁ k₁'
s₂': square (identity_v y₂) (identity_v z₂) k₂ k₂'
s₃: square v₁ v₂ h₁ k₁

transportf_square
  (id_v_right v₂ @ ! id_v_left v₂)
  (id_v_right v₃ @ ! id_v_left v₃) (s₄ ⋆v s₂')
transportf_square
  (idpath (v₁ ·v identity_v x₂) @
   maponpaths (λ z : x₂ -->v x₂, v₁ ·v z)
     (! id_right (identity_v x₂)) @
   maponpaths (λ z : x₂ -->v x₂, v₁ ·v z)
     (id_v_left (identity_v x₂)) @ id_v_right v₁)
  ((maponpaths (λ z : z₂ -->v z₂, v₃ ·v z)
      (! id_left (identity_v z₂)) @
    idpath (v₃ ·v identity_v z₂ · identity_v z₂)) @
   maponpaths (λ z : z₂ -->v z₂, v₃ ·v z)
     (id_v_left (identity_v z₂)) @ id_v_right v₃)
  (transportf_square (idpath (v₁ ·v identity_v x₂))
     (! (maponpaths (λ z : y₂ -->v y₂, v₂ ·v z)
           (! id_left (identity_v y₂)) @
         ! maponpaths (λ z : y₂ -->v y₂, v₂ ·v z)
             (! id_right (identity_v y₂)))) (s₃ ⋆v s₂)
   ⋆h (s₄ ⋆v s₂')) =
transportf_square
  (((id_v_right v₁ @ ! id_v_left v₁) @
    maponpaths (λ z : x₁ -->v x₁, z ·v v₁)
      (! id_right (identity_v x₁))) @
   maponpaths (λ z : x₁ -->v x₁, z ·v v₁)
     (id_v_left (identity_v x₁)) @ id_v_left v₁)
  ((((id_v_right v₃ @ ! id_v_left v₃) @
     maponpaths (λ z : z₁ -->v z₁, z ·v v₃)
       (! id_left (identity_v z₁))) @
    idpath (identity_v z₁ · identity_v z₁ ·v v₃)) @
   maponpaths (λ z : z₁ -->v z₁, z ·v v₃)
     (id_v_left (identity_v z₁)) @ id_v_left v₃)
  (transportf_square (idpath (v₁ ·v identity_v x₂))
     (! (((id_v_right v₂ @ ! id_v_left v₂) @
          maponpaths (λ z : y₁ -->v y₁, z ·v v₂)
            (! id_left (identity_v y₁))) @
         ! ((id_v_right v₂ @ ! id_v_left v₂) @
            maponpaths (λ z : y₁ -->v y₁, z ·v v₂)
              (! id_right (identity_v y₁)))))
     (s₃ ⋆v s₂) ⋆h (s₄ ⋆v s₂'))

⋆h (s₄ ⋆v s₂')

∏
(x₁ x₂ x₃ y₁ y₂
 y₃ : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker)
(h₁
 h₁' : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
       ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧)
(h₂
 h₂' : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
       ⟦ x₂, x₃ ⟧)
(k₁
 k₁' : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
       ⟦ y₁, y₂ ⟧)
(k₂
 k₂' : double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
       ⟦ y₂, y₃ ⟧)
(v₁ : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
        double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
      ⟦ x₁, y₁ ⟧)
(v₂ : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
        double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
      ⟦ x₂, y₂ ⟧)
(v₃ : ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
        double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
      ⟦ x₃, y₃ ⟧) (τ₁ : h₁ ==> h₁') (τ₂ : h₂ ==> h₂')
(θ₁ : k₁ ==> k₁') (θ₂ : k₂ ==> k₂')
(s₁ : square_double_bicat h₁ k₁ v₁ v₂)
(s₁' : square_double_bicat h₁' k₁' v₁ v₂)
(s₂ : square_double_bicat h₂ k₂ v₂ v₃)
(s₂' : square_double_bicat h₂' k₂' v₂ v₃),
is_hor_cylinder s₁ s₁' τ₁ θ₁
→ is_hor_cylinder s₂ s₂' τ₂ θ₂
  → is_hor_cylinder (comp_h_square_bicat s₁ s₂)
      (comp_h_square_bicat s₁' s₂') (τ₂ ⋆⋆ τ₁)
      (θ₂ ⋆⋆ θ₁)
 
C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂, z₁, z₂: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
v₁, v₂: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ x₁,
x₂ ⟧
v₃, h₁: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ x₂,
y₁ ⟧
h₁', h₂: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ y₂, z₁ ⟧
h₂', k₁: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ z₁, z₂ ⟧
k₁': ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
⟦ x₁, y₂ ⟧
k₂: ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
  double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
⟦ x₂, z₁ ⟧
k₂': ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
⟦ y₁, z₂ ⟧
∏ (τ₁ : v₁ ==> v₂) (τ₂ : v₃ ==> h₁) (θ₁ : h₁' ==> h₂)
(θ₂ : h₂' ==> k₁)
(s₁ : square_double_bicat v₁ h₁' k₁' k₂)
(s₁' : square_double_bicat v₂ h₂ k₁' k₂)
(s₂ : square_double_bicat v₃ h₂' k₂ k₂')
(s₂' : square_double_bicat h₁ k₁ k₂ k₂'),
is_hor_cylinder s₁ s₁' τ₁ θ₁
→ is_hor_cylinder s₂ s₂' τ₂ θ₂
  → is_hor_cylinder (comp_h_square_bicat s₁ s₂)
      (comp_h_square_bicat s₁' s₂') (τ₂ ⋆⋆ τ₁)
      (θ₂ ⋆⋆ θ₁)

      
C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂, z₁, z₂: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
v₁, v₂: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ x₁,
x₂ ⟧
v₃, h₁: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ x₂,
y₁ ⟧
h₁', h₂: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ y₂, z₁ ⟧
h₂', k₁: double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker ⟦ z₁, z₂ ⟧
k₁': ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
⟦ x₁, y₂ ⟧
k₂: ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat
  double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
⟦ x₂, z₁ ⟧
k₂': ver_bicat_of_ver_bicat_sq_bicat double_cat_to_ver_bicat_sq_id_comp_whisker
⟦ y₁, z₂ ⟧
p: v₁ ==> v₂
p': v₃ ==> h₁
q: h₁' ==> h₂
q': h₂' ==> k₁
s₁: square_double_bicat v₁ h₁' k₁' k₂
s₁': square_double_bicat v₂ h₂ k₁' k₂
s₂: square_double_bicat v₃ h₂' k₂ k₂'
s₂': square_double_bicat h₁ k₁ k₂ k₂'
r: is_hor_cylinder s₁ s₁' p q
r': is_hor_cylinder s₂ s₂' p' q'
is_hor_cylinder (comp_h_square_bicat s₁ s₂)
  (comp_h_square_bicat s₁' s₂') (p' ⋆⋆ p) (q' ⋆⋆ q)

      
C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂, z₁, z₂: C
v₁, v₂: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
v₃, h₁: C ⟦ x₂, y₁ ⟧
h₁', h₂: C ⟦ y₂, z₁ ⟧
h₂', k₁: C ⟦ z₁, z₂ ⟧
k₁': x₁ -->h y₂
k₂: x₂ -->h z₁
k₂': y₁ -->h z₂
p: v₁ = v₂
p': v₃ = h₁
q: h₁' = h₂
q': h₂' = k₁
s₁: square v₁ h₁' k₁' k₂
s₁': square v₂ h₂ k₁' k₂
s₂: square v₃ h₂' k₂ k₂'
s₂': square h₁ k₁ k₂ k₂'
r: transportf_square (idpath v₁) q s₁ =
transportf_square (! p) (idpath h₂) s₁'
r': transportf_square (idpath v₃) q' s₂ =
transportf_square (! p') (idpath k₁) s₂'
transportf_square (idpath (v₁ · v₃)) (q' ⋆⋆ q)
  (s₁ ⋆v s₂) =
transportf_square (! p' ⋆⋆ p) (idpath (h₂ · k₁))
  (s₁' ⋆v s₂')

      
C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂, z₁, z₂: C
v₁: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
v₃: C ⟦ x₂, y₁ ⟧
h₁': C ⟦ y₂, z₁ ⟧
h₂': C ⟦ z₁, z₂ ⟧
k₁': x₁ -->h y₂
k₂: x₂ -->h z₁
k₂': y₁ -->h z₂
s₁, s₁': square v₁ h₁' k₁' k₂
s₂, s₂': square v₃ h₂' k₂ k₂'
r: transportf_square (idpath v₁) (idpath h₁') s₁ =
transportf_square (! idpath v₁) (idpath h₁') s₁'
r': transportf_square (idpath v₃) (idpath h₂') s₂ =
transportf_square (! idpath v₃) (idpath h₂') s₂'
transportf_square (idpath (v₁ · v₃))
  (idpath h₂' ⋆⋆ idpath h₁') (s₁ ⋆v s₂) =
transportf_square (! idpath v₃ ⋆⋆ idpath v₁)
  (idpath (h₁' · h₂')) (s₁' ⋆v s₂')

      
C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
x₁, x₂, y₁, y₂, z₁, z₂: C
v₁: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
v₃: C ⟦ x₂, y₁ ⟧
h₁': C ⟦ y₂, z₁ ⟧
h₂': C ⟦ z₁, z₂ ⟧

k₂: x₂ -->h z₁
k₂': y₁ -->h z₂
s₁, s₁': square v₁ h₁' k₁' k₂
s₂, s₂': square v₃ h₂' k₂ k₂'
r: s₁ = s₁'
r': s₂ = s₂'
transportf_square (idpath (v₁ · v₃))
  (idpath h₂' ⋆⋆ idpath h₁') (s₁ ⋆v s₂) =
transportf_square (! idpath v₃ ⋆⋆ idpath v₁)
  (idpath (h₁' · h₂')) (s₁' ⋆v s₂')

s₂: square v₃ h₂' k₂ k₂'
s₁ ⋆v s₂ = s₁ ⋆v s₂

      apply idpath.
  Qed.

C: double_cat
ℍ:= horizontal_bicat C: bicat
x, y: C
h₁, h₂: x -->h y
∏ x0 : h₁ ==> h₂,
idfun (square_double_bicat (id_h x) (id_h y) h₁ h₂)
  (vertical_cell_to_square x0) = x0
 abstract
        (intros s ; cbn ;
         refine (maponpaths (transportf_square _ _) (square_id_right_v _) @ _) ;
         unfold transportb_square ;
         rewrite transportf_f_square ;
         apply transportf_square_id).

  (idfun (square_double_bicat (id_h x) (id_h y) h₁ h₂)

         apply transportf_square_id).

(** * 6. Companions and conjoints *)

C: double_cat
x, y: C
h: x -->h y
v: x -->v y
double_cat_are_companions h v ≃ are_companions v h


C: double_cat
x, y: C
h: x -->h y
v: x -->v y
double_cat_are_companions h v ≃ are_companions v h

  
C: double_cat
x, y: C
h: x -->h y
v: x -->v y
∏ x0 : square v (identity_v y) h (identity_h y),
(λ x1 : square v (identity_v y) h (identity_h y),
 ∑ ψ : square (identity_v x) v (identity_h x) h,
 transportf_square (id_v_right (identity_v x))
   (id_v_right (identity_v y))
   (transportf_square (id_v_left (identity_v x))
      (id_v_left (identity_v y))
      (linvunitor_h h ⋆v ψ ⋆h x1) ⋆v runitor_h h) =
 id_v_square h
 × transportf_square (idpath v) (id_right v)
     (transportf_square (id_left v)
        (idpath (v ·v identity_v y)) (ψ ⋆v x1)) =
   id_h_square v) x0
≃ (λ x1 : square v (identity_v y) h (identity_h y),
   ∑ ψ : square_double_bicat (id_h x) v (id_h x) h,
   rwhisker_square (runitor h)
     (lwhisker_square (linvunitor h)
        (comp_v_square_bicat ψ x1)) =
   id_h_square_bicat h
   × dwhisker_square (runitor v)
       (uwhisker_square (linvunitor v)
          (comp_h_square_bicat ψ x1)) =
     id_v_square_bicat v) x0

 abstract
      (intros p ;
       induction p as [ p₁ p₂ ] ;
       refine (p₁ ,, _) ;
       refine (_ @ p₂) ;
       cbn -[transportf_square] ;
       do 2 use transportf_square_eq ;
       apply idpath).

C: double_cat
x, y: C
h: y -->h x
v: x -->v y
∏ x0 : square v (identity_v x) (identity_h x) h,
(λ x1 : square v (identity_v x) (identity_h x) h,
 ∑ ε : square (identity_v y) v h (identity_h y),
 transportf_square (id_v_left (identity_v y))
   (id_v_left (identity_v x))
   (rinvunitor_h h
    ⋆v transportf_square (id_v_right (identity_v y))
         (id_v_right (identity_v x))
         (ε ⋆h x1 ⋆v lunitor_h h)) = id_v_square h
 × transportf_square (idpath v) (id_v_left v)
     (transportf_square (id_v_right v)
        (idpath (identity_v x ·v v)) (x1 ⋆v ε)) =
   id_h_square v) x0
≃ (λ x1 : square v (identity_v x) (identity_h x) h,
   ∑ ε : square_double_bicat (id_h y) v h (id_h y),
   lwhisker_square (rinvunitor h)
     (rwhisker_square (lunitor h)
        (comp_v_square_bicat ε x1)) =
   id_h_square_bicat h
   × dwhisker_square (lunitor v)
       (uwhisker_square (rinvunitor v)
          (comp_h_square_bicat x1 ε)) =
     id_v_square_bicat v) x0

v: x -->v y
φ: square v (identity_v x) (identity_h x) h
ψ: square (identity_v y) v h (identity_h y)
isaprop
  (transportf_square (id_v_left (identity_v y))
     (id_v_left (identity_v x))
     (rinvunitor_h h
      ⋆v transportf_square (id_v_right (identity_v y))
           (id_v_right (identity_v x))
           (ψ ⋆h φ ⋆v lunitor_h h)) = id_v_square h
   × transportf_square (idpath v) (id_v_left v)
       (transportf_square (id_v_right v)
          (idpath (identity_v x ·v v)) (φ ⋆v ψ)) =
     id_h_square v)
C: double_cat
x, y: C
h: y -->h x
v: x -->v y
φ: square v (identity_v x) (identity_h x) h
ψ: square (identity_v y) v h (identity_h y)
isaprop
  (lwhisker_square (rinvunitor h)
     (rwhisker_square (lunitor h)
        (comp_v_square_bicat ψ φ)) =
   id_h_square_bicat h
   × dwhisker_square (lunitor v)
       (uwhisker_square (rinvunitor v)
          (comp_h_square_bicat φ ψ)) =
     id_v_square_bicat v)

v: x -->v y

   ⋆v transportf_square (id_v_right (identity_v y))

    (rwhisker_square (lunitor h)

  id_h_square_bicat h

 abstract
      (intros p ;
       induction p as [ p₁ p₂ ] ;
       refine (p₁ ,, _) ;
       refine (_ @ p₂) ;
       cbn -[transportf_square] ;
       do 2 use transportf_square_eq ;
       apply idpath).
